Back in 2021 when I first transferred to a four year school, I rediscovered your channel after seeing it initially with the Yoshi, Ben 10, Perry, and pre-Covid shenanigans. I watched a few videos before I had to stop due to the overwhelming feeling of FOMO I was getting. I was alone at a new big school and living on my own for the very first time in my life. I was starting from scratch and DYING to have a friend group or even individual friends in general. Seeing you doing EXACTLY what I wanted to do made me restless and drove me to close the tab and put myself out there to make that a reality.  After seeing your goodbye video, I went back and watched ALL of your videos in order. From that, I'm realizing how much I relate to you. Being the friend that cares more about your friends than they do about you, being the friend organizing and getting everyone together, etc. Watching your conversation with your dad was oddly comforting to me. I had felt the same way you did in that video many many times, especially since I transferred to this new school.  Now, I am getting ready to graduate next semester and I'm reflecting on how much I have done with how alone I used to be. I know so many people who start where I was and never leave that place. I always wonder how I was able to make my situation better when so many others have either failed or never tried at all. What made me try in the first place? I think your videos were the catalyst. They proved to me it was possible; my ideal life was already achieved by someone and was well within my reach.  Thank you for doing that for me, Anthony, and for the hours of content that you've given the world. I hope you do something else creative and express it with the world. It would be a shame to lose such a unique, artistic voice that shines so brilliant in a sea of artificiality and mediocrity.
